### 3.2 MessageParam 强类型迁移完成

**已完成**: `MessageParam.java` (sealed interface) + `MessageParamConverter.java` + `LlmProvider.java` 新版 `streamChat()`

**原版对照** — `query.ts` 消息构建核心逻辑:
```typescript
// 原版 query.ts — buildApiMessages() 将内部 Message[] 转换为 API 格式
// 关键逻辑:
// 1. 合并连续的同角色消息 (consecutive same-role messages)
// 2. 去除 thinking blocks (回退模型时)
// 3. 平坦化 tool_use + tool_result 结构
// 4. 处理 system-reminder 标签注入
function buildApiMessages(messages: Message[]): ApiMessage[] {
  return normalize(messages.map(toApiMessage));
}

// 原版 — normalize() 确保消息对满足 API 约束:
// 1. 第一条必须是 user (如果不是，前插空 user)
// 2. user/assistant 严格交替
// 3. 最后一条不能是 assistant (API 要求)
```

**剩余迁移工作**:

> **❗ 源码对齐警告 — MessageParam 现有结构与目标结构不兼容**
>
> 当前 `MessageParam.java` (58行) 使用扁平结构:
> ```java
> // 现有结构 (llm/MessageParam.java)
> sealed interface MessageParam {
>     record UserMessage(String content) implements MessageParam {}
>     record UserMessageWithBlocks(List<Map<String, Object>> contentBlocks) implements MessageParam {}
>     record AssistantMessage(String content, List<ToolUse> toolUses, String thinkingContent) implements MessageParam {}
>     record ToolResultMessage(String toolUseId, String content, boolean isError) implements MessageParam {}
>     record ToolUse(String id, String name, Map<String, Object> input) {}
> }
> ```
>
> 本方案目标结构使用 `ContentPart` 子类型（支持 thinking/redacted_thinking，对齐附录 J 的 `adaptMessages()`）。
> 迁移必须分 3 步渐进执行，不能一次性重写:
>
> **迁移步骤 0a**: 在现有 `MessageParam.java` 中新增 `ContentPart` sealed interface 和新的 record 类型，
>   同时保留旧的 4 个 record 并标记 `@Deprecated`:
> ```java
> // llm/MessageParam.java — 步骤 0a: 新增 ContentPart + 新 record，旧 record 标记 @Deprecated
> public sealed interface MessageParam {
>     String role();
>
>     // ===== 新增: ContentPart 子类型 (对齐附录 J adaptMessages()) =====
>     sealed interface ContentPart {
>         record TextPart(String text) implements ContentPart {}
>         record ToolUsePart(String id, String name, Map<String, Object> input) implements ContentPart {}
>         record ToolResultPart(String toolUseId, String content, boolean isError) implements ContentPart {}
>         record ThinkingPart(String thinking) implements ContentPart {}
>         record RedactedThinkingPart(String data) implements ContentPart {}
>         record ImagePart(String mediaType, String base64Data) implements ContentPart {}
>     }
>
>     // ===== 新版 record (目标结构) =====
>     record UserParam(List<ContentPart> content) implements MessageParam {
>         @Override public String role() { return "user"; }
>     }
>     record AssistantParam(List<ContentPart> content) implements MessageParam {
>         @Override public String role() { return "assistant"; }
>     }
>
>     // ===== 旧版 record (向后兼容，渐进废弃) =====
>     @Deprecated record UserMessage(String content) implements MessageParam { ... }
>     @Deprecated record UserMessageWithBlocks(List<Map<String, Object>> contentBlocks) implements MessageParam { ... }
>     @Deprecated record AssistantMessage(String content, List<ToolUse> toolUses, String thinkingContent) implements MessageParam { ... }
>     @Deprecated record ToolResultMessage(String toolUseId, String content, boolean isError) implements MessageParam { ... }
>     record ToolUse(String id, String name, Map<String, Object> input) {} // 保留、不废弃
> }
> ```
>
> **迁移步骤 0b**: 在 `MessageParamConverter.java` 中新增双向转换:
>   - `fromLegacy(MessageParam.UserMessage)` → `MessageParam.UserParam`
>   - `fromLegacy(MessageParam.AssistantMessage)` → `MessageParam.AssistantParam`
>   当前所有调用方仍使用旧 record，通过 Converter 桥接到新结构。
>
> **迁移步骤 0c**: 逐步将调用方从旧 record 迁移到新 record，顺序:
>   QueryEngine.buildApiMessages() → MessageNormalizer → OpenAiCompatibleProvider → AnthropicProvider
>   每迁移一个调用方后编译验证，确保不破坏现有功能。

| 步骤 | 待迁移代码 | 文件 |
|------|----------|------|
| 1 | `buildApiMessages()` 返回 `List<Map>` → `List<MessageParam>` | `QueryEngine.java` L657-701 |
| 2 | `messageNormalizer.normalize()` 返回 Map → `List<MessageParam>` | `engine/MessageNormalizer.java` |
| 3 | `OpenAiCompatibleProvider` 移除 `toMaps()` 桥接 | `llm/impl/OpenAiCompatibleProvider.java` |
| 4 | 删除 `@deprecated` 旧版 streamChat | `llm/LlmProvider.java` |

**步骤 1**: `buildApiMessages()` 迁移 — 从 `List<Map>` 到 `List<MessageParam>`
```java
// engine/QueryEngine.java — buildApiMessages() 迁移
// 原来: List<Map<String, Object>> buildApiMessages(List<Message> messages)
// 新版: List<MessageParam> buildApiMessages(List<Message> messages)

private List<MessageParam> buildApiMessages(List<Message> messages) {
    List<MessageParam> result = new ArrayList<>();
    for (Message msg : messages) {
        MessageParam param = convertToParam(msg);
        if (param != null) result.add(param);
    }
    // 规范化: 确保 user/assistant 交替 + 第一条为 user
    return messageNormalizer.normalize(result);
}

private MessageParam convertToParam(Message msg) {
    return switch (msg) {
        case Message.UserMessage um -> new MessageParam.UserParam(
            um.content().stream().map(this::convertBlock).toList());
        case Message.AssistantMessage am -> new MessageParam.AssistantParam(
            am.content().stream().map(this::convertBlock).toList());
        default -> null;
    };
}

// ContentBlock → MessageParam.ContentPart 转换
private MessageParam.ContentPart convertBlock(ContentBlock block) {
    return switch (block) {
        case ContentBlock.TextBlock tb ->
            new MessageParam.ContentPart.TextPart(tb.text());
        case ContentBlock.ToolUseBlock tub ->
            new MessageParam.ContentPart.ToolUsePart(
                tub.id(), tub.name(), tub.input());
        case ContentBlock.ToolResultBlock trb ->
            new MessageParam.ContentPart.ToolResultPart(
                trb.toolUseId(), trb.content(), trb.isError());
        case ContentBlock.ThinkingBlock thb ->
            new MessageParam.ContentPart.ThinkingPart(thb.thinking());
        default -> new MessageParam.ContentPart.TextPart(block.toString());
    };
}
```

**步骤 2**: `MessageNormalizer.java` 完整实现

> **与现有代码的关系**: 当前 `MessageNormalizer.java`(343行) 已有 5 阶段管线:
> 过滤 → 转换合并 → thinking处理 → tool配对 → 空消息过滤。
> 以下方案将其扩展为 7 阶段，**新增 Stage 3 (确保首条为 user) 和 Stage 7 (严格交替)**，
> 同时将当前的 `List<Map>` 返回值迁移为 `List<MessageParam>`。
> 当前已有的 5 个阶段逻辑保持不变，仅改变入参/出参类型。
```java
// engine/MessageNormalizer.java — 对齐原版 normalizeMessagesForAPI() 多阶段逻辑
// 技术栈适配说明:
// 原版 normalizeMessagesForAPI() 是一个 ~400 行的复杂函数，包含 10+ 处理阶段
// Java 等价: 拆分为多个 private 方法组成 pipeline，保持可测试性
@Component
public class MessageNormalizer {

    /**
     * 完整规范化管线 (对齐原版 normalizeMessagesForAPI 全流程):
     * 1. 过滤 system/progress/virtual 消息 (原版: filter display-only)
     * 2. 合并连续同角色消息 (原版: mergeUserMessages / mergeAssistantMessages)
     * 3. 确保第一条是 user (原版: API 约束)
     * 4. 处理孤立 thinking-only assistant (原版: filterOrphanedThinkingOnlyMessages)
     * 5. 剪裁末尾 assistant 的 trailing thinking (原版: filterTrailingThinkingFromLastAssistant)
     * 6. 过滤空白 assistant (原版: filterWhitespaceOnlyAssistantMessages)
     * 7. 确保严格交替 (原版: 最终检查)
     *
     * 注意: 原版注释明确指出这些多步规范化 "inherently fragile"，每步可能
     * 创建前一步需要处理的条件。因此顺序很重要，不能随意调整。
     */
    public List<MessageParam> normalize(List<MessageParam> messages) {
        if (messages.isEmpty()) return messages;

        // Stage 1: 过滤不应发送到 API 的消息 (原版: filter progress/system/virtual)
        List<MessageParam> filtered = messages.stream()
            .filter(m -> !(m instanceof MessageParam.SystemParam))  // system 走独立字段
            .toList();

        // Stage 2: 合并连续同角色消息 (对齐原版 consecutive same-role merge)
        List<MessageParam> merged = mergeConsecutiveSameRole(filtered);

        // Stage 3: 确保第一条是 user (对齐原版: 前插空 user 消息)
        if (!merged.isEmpty() && merged.getFirst() instanceof MessageParam.AssistantParam) {
            merged = new ArrayList<>(merged);
            merged.addFirst(new MessageParam.UserParam(
                List.of(new MessageParam.ContentPart.TextPart("[Conversation start]"))));
        }

        // Stage 4: 过滤孤立 thinking-only assistant (原版: filterOrphanedThinkingOnlyMessages)
        // 压缩切片可能产生仅含 thinking block 的 assistant，会导致 API 400
        List<MessageParam> withoutOrphans = filterOrphanedThinkingOnly(merged);

        // Stage 5: 剪裁末尾 assistant 的 trailing thinking (原版: 顺序很重要 — 先 strip thinking，再 filter whitespace)
        List<MessageParam> withoutTrailingThinking = stripTrailingThinkingFromLast(withoutOrphans);

        // Stage 6: 过滤空白内容 assistant (原版: filterWhitespaceOnlyAssistantMessages)
        List<MessageParam> withoutWhitespace = filterWhitespaceOnlyAssistants(withoutTrailingThinking);

        // Stage 7: 最终严格交替检查 (插入占位符)
        return ensureStrictAlternation(withoutWhitespace);
    }

    // --- Stage 2 实现 ---
    private List<MessageParam> mergeConsecutiveSameRole(List<MessageParam> messages) {
        List<MessageParam> result = new ArrayList<>();
        for (MessageParam msg : messages) {
            if (!result.isEmpty() && sameRole(result.getLast(), msg)) {
                MessageParam last = result.removeLast();
                result.add(mergeMessages(last, msg));
            } else {
                result.add(msg);
            }
        }
        return result;
    }

    // --- Stage 4: 过滤仅含 thinking 的孤立 assistant ---
    private List<MessageParam> filterOrphanedThinkingOnly(List<MessageParam> messages) {
        return messages.stream().filter(m -> {
            if (m instanceof MessageParam.AssistantParam ap) {
                return ap.content().stream().anyMatch(
                    p -> !(p instanceof MessageParam.ContentPart.ThinkingPart));
            }
            return true;
        }).toList();
    }

    // --- Stage 5: 剪裁末尾 assistant 的 trailing thinking ---
    private List<MessageParam> stripTrailingThinkingFromLast(List<MessageParam> messages) {
        if (messages.isEmpty()) return messages;
        MessageParam last = messages.getLast();
        if (!(last instanceof MessageParam.AssistantParam ap)) return messages;
        List<MessageParam.ContentPart> stripped = new ArrayList<>(ap.content());
        // 从末尾向前移除 thinking blocks
        while (!stripped.isEmpty()
                && stripped.getLast() instanceof MessageParam.ContentPart.ThinkingPart) {
            stripped.removeLast();
        }
        if (stripped.size() == ap.content().size()) return messages;
        List<MessageParam> result = new ArrayList<>(messages.subList(0, messages.size() - 1));
        if (!stripped.isEmpty()) {
            result.add(new MessageParam.AssistantParam(stripped));
        }
        return result;
    }

    // --- Stage 6: 过滤空白内容 assistant ---
    private List<MessageParam> filterWhitespaceOnlyAssistants(List<MessageParam> messages) {
        return messages.stream().filter(m -> {
            if (m instanceof MessageParam.AssistantParam ap) {
                return ap.content().stream().anyMatch(p -> {
                    if (p instanceof MessageParam.ContentPart.TextPart tp) {
                        return !tp.text().isBlank();
                    }
                    return true;  // 非文本块不过滤
                });
            }
            return true;
        }).toList();
    }

    // --- Stage 7: 严格交替 ---
    private List<MessageParam> ensureStrictAlternation(List<MessageParam> messages) {
        List<MessageParam> result = new ArrayList<>();
        for (MessageParam msg : messages) {
            if (!result.isEmpty() && sameRole(result.getLast(), msg)) {
                if (msg instanceof MessageParam.UserParam) {
                    result.add(new MessageParam.AssistantParam(
                        List.of(new MessageParam.ContentPart.TextPart("[Continue]"))));
                } else {
                    result.add(new MessageParam.UserParam(
                        List.of(new MessageParam.ContentPart.TextPart("[Continue]"))));
                }
            }
            result.add(msg);
        }
        return result;
    }

    /**
     * 从消息列表中移除 thinking blocks (回退模型时使用)。
     * 对齐原版: 回退模型时剥离 thinking blocks 避免 API 报错。
     */
    public List<MessageParam> stripThinkingBlocks(List<MessageParam> messages) {
        return messages.stream().map(msg -> {
            if (msg instanceof MessageParam.AssistantParam ap) {
                List<MessageParam.ContentPart> filtered = ap.content().stream()
                    .filter(p -> !(p instanceof MessageParam.ContentPart.ThinkingPart))
                    .toList();
                return filtered.isEmpty() ? null : new MessageParam.AssistantParam(filtered);
            }
            return msg;
        }).filter(Objects::nonNull).toList();
    }

    // --- 辅助方法 (Stage 2/7 共用) ---
    private boolean sameRole(MessageParam a, MessageParam b) {
        return (a instanceof MessageParam.UserParam && b instanceof MessageParam.UserParam)
            || (a instanceof MessageParam.AssistantParam && b instanceof MessageParam.AssistantParam);
    }

    private MessageParam mergeMessages(MessageParam a, MessageParam b) {
        List<MessageParam.ContentPart> merged = new ArrayList<>();
        if (a instanceof MessageParam.UserParam u1 && b instanceof MessageParam.UserParam u2) {
            merged.addAll(u1.content()); merged.addAll(u2.content());
            return new MessageParam.UserParam(merged);
        }
        if (a instanceof MessageParam.AssistantParam a1 && b instanceof MessageParam.AssistantParam a2) {
            merged.addAll(a1.content()); merged.addAll(a2.content());
            return new MessageParam.AssistantParam(merged);
        }
        return b; // fallback
    }
}
```

**步骤 3**: `OpenAiCompatibleProvider` 移除 `toMaps()` 桥接
```java
// llm/impl/OpenAiCompatibleProvider.java — 直接使用 MessageParam
// 删除旧的 toMaps() 转换方法，直接序列化 MessageParam

private List<Map<String, Object>> serializeMessages(List<MessageParam> params) {
    return params.stream().map(p -> switch (p) {
        case MessageParam.UserParam up -> Map.<String, Object>of(
            "role", "user",
            "content", up.content().stream().map(this::serializePart).toList());
        case MessageParam.AssistantParam ap -> Map.<String, Object>of(
            "role", "assistant",
            "content", ap.content().stream().map(this::serializePart).toList());
    }).toList();
}

private Map<String, Object> serializePart(MessageParam.ContentPart part) {
    return switch (part) {
        case MessageParam.ContentPart.TextPart tp -> Map.of(
            "type", "text", "text", tp.text());
        case MessageParam.ContentPart.ToolUsePart tup -> Map.of(
            "type", "tool_use", "id", tup.id(),
            "name", tup.name(), "input", tup.input());
        case MessageParam.ContentPart.ToolResultPart trp -> Map.of(
            "type", "tool_result", "tool_use_id", trp.toolUseId(),
            "content", trp.content(), "is_error", trp.isError());
        default -> Map.of("type", "text", "text", part.toString());
    };
}
```

**涉及文件**:
- `engine/QueryEngine.java` L657-701 — `buildApiMessages()` 返回 `List<MessageParam>`
- `engine/MessageNormalizer.java` — 完整实现 normalize + stripThinkingBlocks
- `llm/impl/OpenAiCompatibleProvider.java` — 移除 `toMaps()` 桥接，直接序列化 MessageParam
- `llm/LlmProvider.java` — 删除 `@deprecated` 旧版 streamChat

**优先级**: 🟡 P1

---

### 3.3 Anthropic 原生 Provider

**文件**: 新建 `backend/.../llm/impl/AnthropicProvider.java`

> **模型无关性说明**: 此 Provider 仅在 `llm.provider=anthropic` 时激活。
> 当使用 Qwen/OpenAI 时，以下特性通过 `PromptAdapter` (见附录 J) 自动降级:
> - **cache_control**: Qwen/OpenAI 不支持 → PromptAdapter 合并为纯文本，DashScope 有内部自动缓存
> - **extended thinking**: Qwen 不支持 → PromptAdapter 返回 null，可选降级为 COT prompt
> - **独立 system 字段**: Qwen/OpenAI 使用 messages[0].role="system" 代替
> - **redacted_thinking**: Qwen 消息中自动剥离
>
> **SSE 解析策略说明**: 当前 `pom.xml` 已引入 `okhttp-sse` 依赖，
> 但 OkHttp 的 `EventSource` API 不支持 Anthropic SSE 的 `event:` + `data:` 两行序列格式
> （标准 `EventSource` 仅处理 `data:` 行）。因此以下实现手动解析 SSE，
> 而 `OpenAiCompatibleProvider` 可继续使用 `EventSource` API（OpenAI 格式兼容）。

**与 OpenAI 兼容模式的关键差异**:

| 维度 | OpenAI Compatible | Anthropic Native |
|------|-------------------|-------------------|
| system 消息 | messages 数组内 | 独立 `system` 字段 |
| cache_control | 不支持 | `cache_control:{"type":"ephemeral"}` — 费用节省 50-90% |
| thinking | 不支持 | `thinking:{"type":"enabled","budget_tokens":N}` |
| 流格式 | `data: {choices:[{delta:...}]}` | `event: content_block_delta\ndata: {...}` |

**原版对照** — `claude.ts` thinking 配置关键代码:
```typescript
// 原版 claude.ts L1580-1620 — thinking 配置逻辑
if (modelSupportsAdaptiveThinking(options.model)) {
  thinking = { type: 'adaptive' }  // 新模型支持 adaptive
} else {
  let thinkingBudget = getMaxThinkingTokensForModel(options.model);
  thinkingBudget = Math.min(maxOutputTokens - 1, thinkingBudget);
  thinking = { budget_tokens: thinkingBudget, type: 'enabled' };
}
// 关键: thinking 启用时 temperature 必须为 undefined
const temperature = !hasThinking ? (options.temperatureOverride ?? 1) : undefined;
```

**实施步骤**:

**步骤 1**: 新建 `AnthropicProvider.java` — 完整实现
```java
@Service
@ConditionalOnProperty(name = "llm.provider", havingValue = "anthropic")
public class AnthropicProvider implements LlmProvider {

    // 注意: 当前项目仅有 OpenAiCompatibleProvider (使用 matchIfMissing=true)。
    // 此 Provider 仅在显式配置 llm.provider=anthropic 时激活，
    // 两个 Provider 不会同时生效。
    // 如需同时支持多 Provider，应改用 LlmProviderRegistry 动态注册。

    private final OkHttpClient httpClient;
    private final LlmProperties props;
    private final ConcurrentHashMap<String, Call> activeCalls = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
    private final ObjectMapper objectMapper;

    // --- 0. 构造器 + HTTP Client 配置 ---
    // 对齐 OpenAiCompatibleProvider 的连接池和超时配置
    public AnthropicProvider(
            LlmProperties props,
            HttpProperties httpProperties,
            ObjectMapper objectMapper) {
        this.props = props;
        this.objectMapper = objectMapper;
        this.httpClient = new OkHttpClient.Builder()
                .connectionPool(new ConnectionPool(
                        httpProperties.pool().maxIdleConnections(),
                        httpProperties.pool().keepAliveSeconds(),
                        java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit.SECONDS))
                .connectTimeout(Duration.ofSeconds(httpProperties.connectTimeoutSeconds()))
                .readTimeout(Duration.ZERO) // SSE 流式响应: 无读超时
                .writeTimeout(Duration.ofSeconds(httpProperties.writeTimeoutSeconds()))
                .retryOnConnectionFailure(httpProperties.retryOnFailure())
                .addInterceptor(chain -> chain.proceed(
                        chain.request().newBuilder()
                                .header("x-api-key", props.anthropic().apiKey())
                                .header("anthropic-version", "2023-06-01")
                                .header("content-type", "application/json")
                                .build()))
                .build();
    }

    private Request buildHttpRequest(StreamChatRequest request) {
        Map<String, Object> body = buildRequest(
                request.messages(), request.systemSegments(),
                request.model(), request.maxTokens(), request.thinking());
        return new Request.Builder()
                .url(props.anthropic().baseUrl() + "/v1/messages")
                .post(okhttp3.RequestBody.create(
                        objectMapper.writeValueAsBytes(body),
                        MediaType.parse("application/json")))
                .build();
    }

    // --- 1. 请求构建 (对齐原版 buildRequest) ---
    private Map<String, Object> buildRequest(List<MessageParam> messages,
            List<SystemPromptSegment> systemSegments, String model,
            int maxTokens, ThinkingConfig thinking) {
        Map<String, Object> body = new LinkedHashMap<>();
        body.put("model", model);
        body.put("max_tokens", maxTokens);
        body.put("stream", true);

        // system 独立字段 + cache_control (原版 §3.3 关键差异)
        body.put("system", systemSegments.stream().map(seg -> {
            Map<String, Object> block = new LinkedHashMap<>();
            block.put("type", "text");
            block.put("text", seg.content());
            if (seg.cacheable()) {
                block.put("cache_control", Map.of("type", "ephemeral"));
            }
            return block;
        }).toList());

        // messages 转换
        body.put("messages", messages.stream().map(this::toAnthropicMessage).toList());

        // thinking 配置 (对齐原版 claude.ts adaptive vs budget)
        if (thinking != null) {
            if (thinking.isAdaptive()) {
                body.put("thinking", Map.of("type", "adaptive"));
            } else {
                int budget = Math.min(maxTokens - 1, thinking.budgetTokens());
                body.put("thinking", Map.of(
                    "type", "enabled", "budget_tokens", budget));
            }
            // 关键: thinking 启用时不设置 temperature (对齐原版约束)
        } else {
            body.put("temperature", 1.0);
        }

        // 工具定义
        if (!tools.isEmpty()) {
            body.put("tools", tools.stream().map(this::toAnthropicTool).toList());
        }
        return body;
    }

    // --- 2. SSE 解析器 — Anthropic SSE 事件类型 ---
    // 技术栈适配说明:
    // Anthropic SSE 格式与标准 SSE 略有不同:
    //   标准: "data: {json}\n\n"
    //   Anthropic: "event: <type>\ndata: {json}\n\n" (每个数据块前有 event 行)
    // 原版 TS 使用 @anthropic-ai/sdk 的 streaming helper 自动处理
    // Java: 必须手动解析 event: + data: 两行序列
    @Override
    public void streamChat(StreamChatRequest request, StreamChatCallback callback) {
        Request httpReq = buildHttpRequest(request);
        Call call = httpClient.newCall(httpReq);
        activeCalls.put(request.sessionId(), call);

        try (Response response = call.execute()) {
            // 检查 HTTP 状态码 (原版 SDK 自动处理，Java 需手动检查)
            if (!response.isSuccessful()) {
                String body = response.body() != null ? response.body().string() : "";
                int code = response.code();
                // 对齐原版错误分类: 413=prompt_too_long, 429=rate_limit, 529=overloaded
                boolean retryable = code == 429 || code == 529 || code == 503;
                callback.onError(new LlmApiException(body, retryable, code));
                return;
            }

            BufferedSource source = response.body().source();
            String currentBlockType = null;
            int currentBlockIndex = -1;
            String pendingEventType = null;  // 缓存 event: 行的类型

            while (!source.exhausted()) {
                String line = source.readUtf8Line();
                if (line == null || line.isEmpty()) {
                    pendingEventType = null;  // 空行 = 事件边界
                    continue;
                }
                // Anthropic SSE: event: 行在 data: 行之前
                if (line.startsWith("event: ")) {
                    pendingEventType = line.substring(7).trim();
                    continue;
                }
                if (!line.startsWith("data: ")) continue;
                String json = line.substring(6);

                // 特殊处理: error 事件 (原版 SDK 会将其转为异常)
                if ("error".equals(pendingEventType)) {
                    JsonNode errorEvent = objectMapper.readTree(json);
                    String errorType = errorEvent.path("error").path("type").asText("unknown");
                    String errorMsg = errorEvent.path("error").path("message").asText();
                    boolean retryable = "overloaded_error".equals(errorType)
                        || "rate_limit_error".equals(errorType);
                    callback.onError(new LlmApiException(errorMsg, retryable, 0));
                    return;
                }

                JsonNode event = objectMapper.readTree(json);
                String eventType = event.has("type") ? event.get("type").asText()
                    : (pendingEventType != null ? pendingEventType : "unknown");

                switch (eventType) {
                    // 事件 1: message_start → 初始化
                    case "message_start" -> {
                        callback.onEvent(new LlmStreamEvent.MessageStart(
                            event.at("/message/id").asText()));
                    }
                    // 事件 2: content_block_start → 新内容块
                    case "content_block_start" -> {
                        currentBlockIndex = event.get("index").asInt();
                        JsonNode block = event.get("content_block");
                        currentBlockType = block.get("type").asText();
                        switch (currentBlockType) {
                            case "text" -> callback.onEvent(
                                new LlmStreamEvent.TextStart(currentBlockIndex));
                            case "tool_use" -> callback.onEvent(
                                new LlmStreamEvent.ToolUseStart(
                                    block.get("id").asText(),
                                    block.get("name").asText()));
                            case "thinking" -> callback.onEvent(
                                new LlmStreamEvent.ThinkingStart(currentBlockIndex));
                        }
                    }
                    // 事件 3: content_block_delta → 增量内容
                    case "content_block_delta" -> {
                        JsonNode delta = event.get("delta");
                        String deltaType = delta.get("type").asText();
                        switch (deltaType) {
                            case "text_delta" -> callback.onEvent(
                                new LlmStreamEvent.TextDelta(delta.get("text").asText()));
                            case "input_json_delta" -> callback.onEvent(
                                new LlmStreamEvent.ToolInputDelta(
                                    delta.get("partial_json").asText()));
                            case "thinking_delta" -> callback.onEvent(
                                new LlmStreamEvent.ThinkingDelta(
                                    delta.get("thinking").asText()));
                        }
                    }
                    // 事件 4: content_block_stop → 内容块结束
                    case "content_block_stop" -> {
                        callback.onEvent(new LlmStreamEvent.BlockStop(currentBlockIndex));
                    }
                    // 事件 5: message_delta → usage + stop_reason
                    case "message_delta" -> {
                        JsonNode delta = event.get("delta");
                        String stopReason = delta.has("stop_reason")
                            ? delta.get("stop_reason").asText() : null;
                        JsonNode usage = event.get("usage");
                        callback.onEvent(new LlmStreamEvent.MessageDelta(
                            stopReason,
                            usage != null ? usage.get("output_tokens").asInt() : 0));
                    }
                    // 事件 6: message_stop → 流结束
                    case "message_stop" -> {
                        callback.onComplete();
                    }
                }
            }
        } catch (IOException e) {
            if (call.isCanceled()) {
                callback.onComplete(); // abort 导致的取消
            } else {
                callback.onError(e);
            }
        } finally {
            activeCalls.remove(request.sessionId());
        }
    }

    // --- 3. Abort 支持 ---
    @Override
    public void abortStream(String sessionId) {
        Call call = activeCalls.remove(sessionId);
        if (call != null) call.cancel();
    }

    // --- 4. ThinkingConfig ---
    public record ThinkingConfig(boolean adaptive, int budgetTokens) {
        public boolean isAdaptive() { return adaptive; }
        public static ThinkingConfig adaptive() { return new ThinkingConfig(true, 0); }
        public static ThinkingConfig budget(int tokens) { return new ThinkingConfig(false, tokens); }
    }
}
```

**步骤 2**: SSE 事件类型定义
```java
// llm/LlmStreamEvent.java — Anthropic SSE 事件类型
public sealed interface LlmStreamEvent {
    record MessageStart(String messageId) implements LlmStreamEvent {}
    record TextStart(int index) implements LlmStreamEvent {}
    record TextDelta(String text) implements LlmStreamEvent {}
    record ToolUseStart(String id, String name) implements LlmStreamEvent {}
    record ToolInputDelta(String partialJson) implements LlmStreamEvent {}
    record ThinkingStart(int index) implements LlmStreamEvent {}
    record ThinkingDelta(String thinking) implements LlmStreamEvent {}
    record BlockStop(int index) implements LlmStreamEvent {}
    record MessageDelta(String stopReason, int outputTokens) implements LlmStreamEvent {}
}
```

**步骤 3**: 配置
```yaml
llm:
  provider: anthropic
  anthropic:
    api-key: ${ANTHROPIC_API_KEY}
    base-url: https://api.anthropic.com
    default-model: claude-sonnet-4-20250514
    thinking:
      enabled: true
      mode: adaptive  # adaptive | budget
      budget-tokens: 10000
```

**涉及文件**:
- `llm/impl/AnthropicProvider.java` — 新建 (包含完整 SSE 解析 + thinking + cache_control)
- `llm/LlmStreamEvent.java` — 新建 sealed interface
- `config/LlmProperties.java` — 新增 anthropic 配置项

**优先级**: 🟡 P1

### 3.4 WebSocket TODO-3~7 接入

以下 5 个 Client→Server 端点仅有日志打印，需接入业务逻辑:

**步骤 0**: 定义完整 Payload Record (当前缺失)

> **依赖前提**: 当前 `pom.xml` 缺少 Jakarta Validation 依赖，必须先添加:
> ```xml
> <dependency>
>     <groupId>org.springframework.boot</groupId>
>     <artifactId>spring-boot-starter-validation</artifactId>
> </dependency>
> ```
> 否则 `@NotBlank`/`@Pattern` 等注解无法编译。

> **技术栈适配说明**: 原版 TypeScript 使用 Zod schema 验证 WebSocket 消息 payload，
> 在 Java + Spring STOMP 中，payload 由 Jackson 反序列化——compact constructor 中
> 抛出的异常会导致反序列化失败（MappingException），客户端只收到不可读的 500 错误。
> 正确做法是使用 **Jakarta Validation 注解** + Spring 的 `@Validated` 支持，
> 结合 `@MessageExceptionHandler` 统一处理验证错误并返回友好提示。
> compact constructor 仅保留 null→default 赋值（不可变 record 的规范化场景）。

```java
// websocket/payload/ — 5 个 Client→Server 请求 Payload
// 技术栈适配: TS Zod schema → Java Jakarta Validation + Jackson 反序列化
import jakarta.validation.constraints.*;

/** TODO-3: 切换模型 */
public record ModelChangePayload(
    @NotBlank(message = "model must not be blank")
    String model
) {}
// 注意: model 合法性用自定义 @SupportedModel 注解或在 Service 层校验,
// 避免在 record 构造器中耦合 ModelRegistry (反序列化时 Spring 上下文未注入)

/** TODO-4: 切换权限模式 */
public record PermissionModePayload(
    @NotBlank(message = "mode must not be blank")
    @Pattern(regexp = "(?i)DEFAULT|PLAN|ACCEPT_EDITS|DONT_ASK|BYPASS_PERMISSIONS",
             message = "Invalid permission mode. Allowed: DEFAULT, PLAN, ACCEPT_EDITS, DONT_ASK, BYPASS_PERMISSIONS")
    String mode
) {}
// 注意: 仅允许 5 个外部模式，AUTO 和 BUBBLE 为内部模式，不应由客户端设置

/** TODO-5: Slash 命令执行 */
public record CommandPayload(
    @NotBlank String command,    // 命令名 (如 "commit", "review")
    String args,                 // 命令参数 (可为 null)
    String sessionId             // 会话 ID (可由后端从 STOMP header 提取)
) {}

/** TODO-6: MCP 操作 */
public record McpOperationPayload(
    @NotBlank
    @Pattern(regexp = "connect|disconnect|refresh|list",
             message = "Invalid MCP operation, allowed: connect/disconnect/refresh/list")
    String operation,
    String serverId    // MCP 服务器 ID (connect/disconnect 时必填, 在 Service 层校验)
) {}

/** TODO-7: 文件回退 */
public record RewindPayload(
    @NotBlank(message = "messageId must not be blank")
    String messageId,
    List<String> filePaths  // 要回退的文件列表 (空则回退所有)
) {
    // compact constructor 仅做 null→default 规范化 (不抛异常)
    public RewindPayload {
        if (filePaths == null) filePaths = List.of();
    }
}

// ──── 统一验证错误处理 (WebSocketController 内) ────
// 技术栈适配: TS try/catch → Spring @MessageExceptionHandler
@MessageExceptionHandler(MethodArgumentNotValidException.class)
@SendToUser("/queue/errors")
public Map<String, Object> handleValidationError(MethodArgumentNotValidException ex) {
    String message = ex.getBindingResult().getFieldErrors().stream()
        .map(fe -> fe.getField() + ": " + fe.getDefaultMessage())
        .collect(Collectors.joining("; "));
    return Map.of("type", "VALIDATION_ERROR", "message", message);
}
```

        SimpMessageHeaderAccessor headers) {

        SimpMessageHeaderAccessor headers) {

#### TODO-5: Slash 命令 `/app/command` (L512-519)
```java
@MessageMapping("/command")
public void handleCommand(@Validated @Payload CommandPayload payload,
        SimpMessageHeaderAccessor headers) {
    String sessionId = extractSessionId(headers);
    try {
        CommandRegistry.CommandResult cmdResult = commandRegistry.execute(
            payload.command(), payload.args(), sessionId);
        if (cmdResult.hasOutput()) {
            push(sessionId, "command_result", Map.of(
                "command", payload.command(), "output", cmdResult.output()));
        }
        // 某些命令可能触发 query (如 /commit 需要 AI 生成 commit message)
        if (cmdResult.triggersQuery()) {
            queryEngine.submitQuery(sessionId, cmdResult.queryPrompt());
        }
    } catch (CommandNotFoundException e) {
        push(sessionId, "error", Map.of(
            "message", "Unknown command: /" + payload.command(),
            "code", "COMMAND_NOT_FOUND"));
    }
}
```

#### TODO-6: MCP 操作 `/app/mcp` (L524-531)
```java
@MessageMapping("/mcp")
public void handleMcpOperation(@Validated @Payload McpOperationPayload payload,
        SimpMessageHeaderAccessor headers) {
    String sessionId = extractSessionId(headers);
    switch (payload.operation()) {
        case "connect"    -> mcpClientManager.connect(payload.serverId());
        case "disconnect" -> mcpClientManager.disconnect(payload.serverId());
        case "refresh"    -> mcpClientManager.refreshTools(payload.serverId());
        case "list"       -> push(sessionId, "mcp_status",
            Map.of("servers", mcpClientManager.listServers()));
    }
}
```

#### TODO-7: 文件回退 `/app/rewind` (L536-543)
```java
@MessageMapping("/rewind")
public void handleRewind(@Validated @Payload RewindPayload payload,
        SimpMessageHeaderAccessor headers) {
    String sessionId = extractSessionId(headers);
    List<String> restoredFiles = new ArrayList<>();
    List<String> targets = payload.filePaths().isEmpty()
        ? fileHistoryService.getAffectedFiles(sessionId, payload.messageId())
        : payload.filePaths();
    for (String filePath : targets) {
        fileHistoryService.getSnapshot(sessionId, payload.messageId(), filePath)
            .ifPresent(snap -> {
                try {
                    Files.writeString(Path.of(filePath), snap.content());
                    restoredFiles.add(filePath);
                } catch (IOException e) {
                    log.error("Failed to rewind file: {}", filePath, e);
                }
            });
    }
    push(sessionId, "rewind_complete", Map.of(
        "messageId", payload.messageId(),
        "files", restoredFiles));
}
```

**涉及文件**:
- `backend/pom.xml` — **新增依赖** `spring-boot-starter-validation`（否则 @NotBlank/@Pattern 注解无法编译）
- `websocket/WebSocketController.java` — 5 个 TODO 端点接入业务逻辑 + 新增 `@MessageExceptionHandler`
- `websocket/payload/*.java` — 新建 5 个类型安全 Payload record
- 各对应 Service (SessionManager/CommandRegistry/McpClientManager/FileHistoryService)

**优先级**: 🟡 P1

### 3.5 敏感信息过滤

**新建**: `backend/.../security/SensitiveDataFilter.java`

```java
@Component
public class SensitiveDataFilter {
    private static final List<Pattern> PATTERNS = List.of(
        Pattern.compile("(sk-[a-zA-Z0-9]{20,})"),                    // OpenAI
        Pattern.compile("(AKIA[0-9A-Z]{16})"),                       // AWS
        Pattern.compile("(ghp_[a-zA-Z0-9]{36})"),                    // GitHub
        Pattern.compile("(?i)(api[_-]?key|secret|password|token|auth)\\s*[=:]\\s*['\"]?([^\\s'\"]{8,})"),
        Pattern.compile("(eyJ[a-zA-Z0-9_-]{10,}\\.[a-zA-Z0-9_-]{10,}\\.[a-zA-Z0-9_-]{10,})"), // JWT
        Pattern.compile("-----BEGIN (RSA |EC |DSA )?PRIVATE KEY-----")
    );

    public String filter(String content) {
        if (content == null) return null;
        String result = content;
        for (Pattern p : PATTERNS) result = p.matcher(result).replaceAll("***REDACTED***");
        return result;
    }
}
```

**接入点** — `ToolExecutionPipeline.java` 阶段 6:
```java
if (result.content() != null) {
    String filtered = sensitiveDataFilter.filter(result.content());
    if (!filtered.equals(result.content()))
        result = new ToolResult(filtered, result.isError(), result.metadata());
}
```

**涉及文件**:
- `security/SensitiveDataFilter.java` — 新建
- `tool/ToolExecutionPipeline.java` — 添加过滤阶段

**优先级**: 🟡 P1

### 3.6 ToolResultBudget 截断策略修复

**问题** (来自三向对照审查): `SnipService.snipToolResults()` 使用简单截尾策略，原版保留头尾中间插入截断标记。

**原版对照** — `toolLimits.ts` 完整限制常量:
```typescript
// 原版 toolLimits.ts — 四层截断策略常量
export const DEFAULT_MAX_RESULT_SIZE_CHARS = 50_000;    // 单工具结果 > 此值 → 持久化到磁盘
export const MAX_TOOL_RESULT_TOKENS = 100_000;           // 单工具结果 token 上限
export const BYTES_PER_TOKEN = 4;                        // token-byte 估算比
export const MAX_TOOL_RESULT_BYTES = MAX_TOOL_RESULT_TOKENS * BYTES_PER_TOKEN; // 400KB
export const MAX_TOOL_RESULTS_PER_MESSAGE_CHARS = 200_000; // 单消息内所有 tool_result 总和上限
export const TOOL_SUMMARY_MAX_LENGTH = 50;

// 原版 toolResultStorage.ts — 大结果持久化逻辑
const TOOL_RESULT_CLEARED_MESSAGE = '[Old tool result content cleared]';
const PERSISTED_OUTPUT_TAG = '<persisted-output>'; // 大结果保存到文件后的标记
```

**修复** — 对齐原版四层截断策略:
```java
// engine/SnipService.java — 对齐原版截断策略

// 常量 (对齐原版 toolLimits.ts)
private static final int DEFAULT_MAX_RESULT_SIZE_CHARS = 50_000;
private static final int MAX_TOOL_RESULT_TOKENS = 100_000;
private static final int BYTES_PER_TOKEN = 4;
private static final int MAX_TOOL_RESULT_BYTES = MAX_TOOL_RESULT_TOKENS * BYTES_PER_TOKEN;
private static final int MAX_TOOL_RESULTS_PER_MESSAGE_CHARS = 200_000;
private static final String TRUNCATION_MARKER = "\n\n[... content truncated (%d/%d chars) ...]\n\n";
private static final String PERSISTED_OUTPUT_TAG = "<persisted-output>";

// --- 策略 1: 单工具结果截断 (保留头尾) ---
public String snipToolResult(String content, int maxChars) {
    if (content == null || content.length() <= maxChars) return content;
    int headSize = (int) (maxChars * 0.5);  // 前 50%
    int tailSize = maxChars - headSize - 80; // 后 ~50% (预留标记空间)
    return content.substring(0, headSize)
        + String.format(TRUNCATION_MARKER, content.length(), maxChars)
        + content.substring(content.length() - tailSize);
}

// --- 策略 2: 单消息内多工具结果总和限制 (对齐原版 MAX_TOOL_RESULTS_PER_MESSAGE_CHARS) ---
public List<ContentBlock> budgetToolResults(List<ContentBlock> blocks) {
    int totalChars = blocks.stream()
        .filter(b -> b instanceof ContentBlock.ToolResultBlock)
        .mapToInt(b -> ((ContentBlock.ToolResultBlock) b).content().length())
        .sum();
    if (totalChars <= MAX_TOOL_RESULTS_PER_MESSAGE_CHARS) return blocks;

    // 按大小降序，对最大的结果依次持久化到磁盘
    List<ContentBlock.ToolResultBlock> sorted = blocks.stream()
        .filter(b -> b instanceof ContentBlock.ToolResultBlock)
        .map(b -> (ContentBlock.ToolResultBlock) b)
        .sorted(Comparator.comparingInt(b -> -b.content().length()))
        .toList();
    Set<String> persistedIds = new HashSet<>();
    int running = totalChars;
    for (ContentBlock.ToolResultBlock trb : sorted) {
        if (running <= MAX_TOOL_RESULTS_PER_MESSAGE_CHARS) break;
        persistedIds.add(trb.toolUseId());
        running -= trb.content().length();
        // 保存到磁盘
        persistToolResult(trb.toolUseId(), trb.content());
    }
    // 替换已持久化的结果为预览 + 文件路径
    return blocks.stream().map(b -> {
        if (b instanceof ContentBlock.ToolResultBlock trb
                && persistedIds.contains(trb.toolUseId())) {
            String preview = snipToolResult(trb.content(), 200);
            return ContentBlock.toolResult(trb.toolUseId(),
                preview + "\n" + PERSISTED_OUTPUT_TAG + getPersistedPath(trb.toolUseId()),
                false);
        }
        return b;
    }).toList();
}
```

**涉及文件**: `engine/SnipService.java`

**优先级**: 🟡 P1

---

### 3.7 权限管线 Step 1f 补全

**问题** (来自三向对照审查): 新版缺少内容级 ask 规则检查（针对 BashTool 命令内容匹配），bypass 模式下可能跳过对特定命令的额外确认。

**原版对照** — `bashPermissions.ts` 内容级规则关键逻辑:
```typescript
// 原版 bashPermissions.ts — 裸 Shell 前缀黑名单 (禁止生成建议规则)
const BARE_SHELL_PREFIXES = new Set([
  'sh', 'bash', 'zsh', 'fish', 'csh', 'tcsh', 'ksh', 'dash',
  'cmd', 'powershell', 'pwsh',
  'env', 'xargs',            // 可包装任意命令
  'nice', 'stdbuf', 'nohup', 'timeout', 'time', // 可包装任意命令
  'sudo', 'doas', 'pkexec',  // 权限提升
]);

// 原版 — 建议规则生成: 提取前 2 个词作为前缀
function getSimpleCommandPrefix(command: string): string | null {
  // 解析命令，跳过环境变量赋值，提取前 2 个词
  // 如 "git commit -m 'msg'" → "git commit"
  // 如 "ENV=1 python3 script.py" → "python3" (跳过 ENV=1)
  return remaining.slice(0, 2).join(' ');
}

// 原版 — heredoc 和多行命令的特殊处理
function suggestionForExactCommand(command: string) {
  const heredocPrefix = extractPrefixBeforeHeredoc(command);
  if (heredocPrefix) return sharedSuggestionForPrefix(BashTool.name, heredocPrefix);
  if (command.includes('\n')) {
    const firstLine = command.split('\n')[0].trim();
    if (firstLine) return sharedSuggestionForPrefix(BashTool.name, firstLine);
  }
  // ...
}
```

**修复** — 在 `PermissionPipeline.java` Step 1c 之后补充内容级 ask 规则:
```java
// permission/PermissionPipeline.java — Step 1f 内容级 ask 规则

// 裸 Shell 前缀黑名单 (对齐原版 BARE_SHELL_PREFIXES)
private static final Set<String> BARE_SHELL_PREFIXES = Set.of(
    "sh", "bash", "zsh", "fish", "csh", "tcsh", "ksh", "dash",
    "cmd", "powershell", "pwsh",
    "env", "xargs",
    "nice", "stdbuf", "nohup", "timeout", "time",
    "sudo", "doas", "pkexec"
);

// 内容级危险模式 (即使 bypass 也强制 ask)
private static final List<Pattern> CONTENT_LEVEL_ASK_PATTERNS = List.of(
    Pattern.compile("rm\\s+(-[rRf]+\\s+)*(/|~|\\$HOME)"),           // rm -rf / 或 ~
    Pattern.compile("chmod\\s+(-R\\s+)?777\\s+/"),                    // chmod -R 777 /
    Pattern.compile(">(\\s*)/dev/sd[a-z]"),                            // 覆写磁盘设备
    Pattern.compile("mkfs\\."),                                        // 格式化文件系统
    Pattern.compile("dd\\s+.*of=/dev/"),                               // dd 写入设备
    Pattern.compile(":(){ :\\|:& };:"),                                // fork bomb
    Pattern.compile("git\\s+push\\s+.*--force"),                       // git push --force
    Pattern.compile("git\\s+(reset|clean)\\s+--hard"),                 // git reset --hard
    Pattern.compile("DROP\\s+(TABLE|DATABASE)", Pattern.CASE_INSENSITIVE) // SQL DROP
);

// 在 checkPermission() 中，Step 1c 之后插入:
private PermissionDecision checkContentLevelAsk(Tool tool, Map<String, Object> input) {
    if (!"BashTool".equals(tool.getName())) return null;
    String command = (String) input.get("command");
    if (command == null) return null;

    // 检查 1: 裸 shell 前缀 (对齐原版 BARE_SHELL_PREFIXES)
    String firstWord = command.trim().split("\\s+")[0];
    if (BARE_SHELL_PREFIXES.contains(firstWord)) {
        return PermissionDecision.ask(
            "Shell wrapper '" + firstWord + "' can execute arbitrary commands",
            List.of());
    }

    // 检查 2: 内容级危险模式
    for (Pattern pattern : CONTENT_LEVEL_ASK_PATTERNS) {
        if (pattern.matcher(command).find()) {
            return PermissionDecision.ask(
                "Dangerous command pattern detected: " + pattern.pattern(),
                List.of());
        }
    }
    return null; // 未命中，继续正常流程
}
```

**涉及文件**: `permission/PermissionPipeline.java`

**优先级**: 🟡 P1

---

### 3.8 连接状态指示器

**问题**: `useWebSocket.ts` 缺少连接状态同步到 UI Store，前端无法显示实时连接状态。另缺少重连递增退避、心跳超时检测、连接计数。

**实施步骤**:

**步骤 1**: 增强 `useWebSocket.ts` — 连接状态同步 + 重连递增退避
```typescript
// hooks/useWebSocket.ts — 增强版本
// 新增: 状态同步到 BridgeStore + 重连递增退避 + 心跳超时检测
//
// 技术栈适配说明:
// 1. @stomp/stompjs 的 Client 不直接暴露 pong 帧回调，心跳监控通过
//    `onWebSocketClose` + `forcedReconnectDelay` 实现，不能假设有 dispatch pong 消息。
// 2. 去掉 SockJS 依赖 (对齐 P2-5)，使用原生 WebSocket。
// 3. STOMP 库内置心跳机制已经监控 pong，但不会触发回调，
//    因此用 `forcedReconnectDelay` 作为心跳超时的备用机制。

import { useBridgeStore } from '@/store/bridgeStore';
import { useNotificationStore } from '@/store/notificationStore';

// 重连递增退避参数
const RECONNECT_DELAYS = [1000, 2000, 5000, 10000, 30000]; // 最大 30s
let reconnectAttempt = 0;

// 在 Client 配置中增强:
const client = new Client({
    // 技术栈适配: 去掉 SockJS，使用原生 WebSocket
    // 原: webSocketFactory: () => new SockJS('/ws')
    // 现代浏览器均支持原生 WS，SockJS 引入额外 HTTP fallback 开销
    brokerURL: `${window.location.protocol === 'https:' ? 'wss:' : 'ws:'}//${window.location.host}/ws`,

    reconnectDelay: 0, // 禁用内置重连，使用自定义递增退避
    heartbeatIncoming: 4000,
    heartbeatOutgoing: 4000,
    // 技术栈适配: @stomp/stompjs 不暴露 pong 回调，但内置心跳检测在
    // forcedReconnectDelay ms 内无 pong 会自动断开并触发 onWebSocketClose
    forcedReconnectDelay: 15000, // 15s 无响应强制断开

    onConnect: () => {
        reconnectAttempt = 0; // 连接成功重置计数器

        // 同步状态到 BridgeStore
        useBridgeStore.getState().updateBridgeStatus({
            status: 'connected',
            url: window.location.origin,
            connectedAt: Date.now(),
        });

        // 清除断连通知
        useNotificationStore.getState().removeNotification('ws-disconnected');

        // 订阅 + 消息分发 (... 已有逻辑)
        optionsRef.current.onConnect?.();
    },

    onDisconnect: () => {
        useBridgeStore.getState().updateBridgeStatus({
            status: 'disconnected', url: '',
        });
        optionsRef.current.onDisconnect?.();

        // 自定义重连 (递增退避)
        scheduleReconnect();
    },

    // 技术栈适配: onWebSocketClose 是 @stomp/stompjs 检测心跳失败后的回调
    // 原版 TS 通过 AbortController.signal 监控连接状态，这里用 onWebSocketClose 替代
    onWebSocketClose: (evt) => {
        console.warn('[WebSocket] Connection closed:', evt.code, evt.reason);
        // forcedReconnectDelay 超时断开也会触发此回调
    },

    onStompError: (frame) => {
        useBridgeStore.getState().updateBridgeStatus({
            status: 'error',
            url: '',
            error: frame.headers['message'] || 'STOMP error',
        });
        useNotificationStore.getState().addNotification({
            key: 'ws-error',
            level: 'error',
            message: `WebSocket 错误: ${frame.headers['message'] || 'Unknown'}`,
            timeout: 10000,
        });
        optionsRef.current.onError?.(new Error(frame.headers['message']));
    },
});

// 递增退避重连
function scheduleReconnect() {
    const delay = RECONNECT_DELAYS[Math.min(reconnectAttempt, RECONNECT_DELAYS.length - 1)];
    reconnectAttempt++;
    useBridgeStore.getState().updateBridgeStatus({
        status: 'reconnecting',
        url: '',
        nextRetryAt: Date.now() + delay,
        attempt: reconnectAttempt,
    });
    useNotificationStore.getState().addNotification({
        key: 'ws-disconnected',
        level: 'warning',
        message: `连接断开，${delay / 1000}s 后重连 (第 ${reconnectAttempt} 次)`,
        persistent: true,
    });
    setTimeout(() => {
        if (!globalClient?.active) {
            globalClient?.activate();
        }
    }, delay);
}
```

**步骤 2**: `ConnectionIndicator.tsx` 状态指示器组件
```typescript
// components/status/ConnectionIndicator.tsx
import { useBridgeStore } from '@/store/bridgeStore';

export const ConnectionIndicator: React.FC = () => {
    const { status, attempt, nextRetryAt } = useBridgeStore(
        s => ({ status: s.bridgeStatus?.status, attempt: s.bridgeStatus?.attempt,
                nextRetryAt: s.bridgeStatus?.nextRetryAt }));

    const statusConfig = {
        connected:    { color: 'bg-green-500', label: '已连接', pulse: false },
        disconnected: { color: 'bg-red-500', label: '已断开', pulse: false },
        reconnecting: { color: 'bg-yellow-500', label: `重连中 #${attempt}`, pulse: true },
        error:        { color: 'bg-red-600', label: '错误', pulse: true },
    };
    const cfg = statusConfig[status || 'disconnected'];

    return (
        <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 text-xs text-gray-500">
            <span className={`w-2 h-2 rounded-full ${cfg.color} ${cfg.pulse ? 'animate-pulse' : ''}`} />
            <span>{cfg.label}</span>
        </div>
    );
};
```

**涉及文件**:
- `frontend/src/hooks/useWebSocket.ts` — 增强重连递增退避 + 心跳监控 + 状态同步
- `frontend/src/components/status/ConnectionIndicator.tsx` — 新建状态指示器
- `frontend/src/store/bridgeStore.ts` — 新增 reconnecting/attempt/nextRetryAt 字段

**优先级**: 🟡 P1

## 四、第三阶段：用户体验与质量提升

> 本阶段提升用户交互体验、安全规则覆盖度和测试质量。

### 4.1 工具结果分化渲染

**现状**: `ToolCallBlock.tsx` (202行) 所有工具结果统一 `CodeBlock` 渲染。

**实施步骤**:

**步骤 1**: 新建 4 个专用渲染器

```typescript
// renderers/TerminalRenderer.tsx — BashTool 专用渲染器
// 功能: ANSI 转义码解析 + stdout/stderr 分色 + 可折叠 + 复制按钮
//
// 技术栈适配说明:
// ansi-to-html 输出含 HTML 标签 (如 <span style="color:...">) 必须经过
// DOMPurify 清洗后才能放入 dangerouslySetInnerHTML。
// escapeXML:true 只转义 XML 实体 (&<>") 但不能防御所有 XSS 向量。
// 原版 TS 使用 terminal UI 组件 (ink) 不涉及 HTML 注入，但 Web 版必须额外防护。
import React, { useMemo, useState } from 'react';
import Convert from 'ansi-to-html';
import DOMPurify from 'dompurify';

// 技术栈适配: 配置 DOMPurify 仅允许 ansi-to-html 生成的安全标签
const PURIFY_CONFIG = {
    ALLOWED_TAGS: ['span', 'b', 'i', 'u'],
    ALLOWED_ATTR: ['style', 'class'],
    // 禁止事件属性和危险协议
    FORBID_ATTR: ['onerror', 'onclick', 'onload'],
};

const ansiConverter = new Convert({ newline: true, escapeXML: true });

interface TerminalRendererProps {
    content: string;
    exitCode?: number;
    isError?: boolean;
    maxLines?: number;  // 超过此行数自动折叠
}

export const TerminalRenderer: React.FC<TerminalRendererProps> = ({
    content, exitCode, isError, maxLines = 50,
}) => {
    const [expanded, setExpanded] = useState(false);
    const lines = content.split('\n');
    const shouldCollapse = lines.length > maxLines;
    const displayContent = shouldCollapse && !expanded
        ? lines.slice(0, maxLines).join('\n') + `\n... (${lines.length - maxLines} more lines)`
        : content;

    // 技术栈适配: ansi-to-html 输出 → DOMPurify 清洗 → dangerouslySetInnerHTML
    // 两步缓存: useMemo 避免重复转换 + 清洗
    const html = useMemo(
        () => DOMPurify.sanitize(ansiConverter.toHtml(displayContent), PURIFY_CONFIG),
        [displayContent]
    );

    return (
        <div className="relative group">
            <div className={`font-mono text-sm p-3 rounded-md overflow-x-auto
                ${isError || (exitCode && exitCode !== 0)
                    ? 'bg-red-950/30 border border-red-800/50'
                    : 'bg-gray-900 text-gray-100'}`}>
                {/* 退出码标签 */}
                {exitCode !== undefined && (
                    <span className={`absolute top-2 right-2 text-xs px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded
                        ${exitCode === 0 ? 'bg-green-800 text-green-200' : 'bg-red-800 text-red-200'}`}>
                        exit {exitCode}
                    </span>
                )}
                <pre dangerouslySetInnerHTML={{ __html: html }} className="whitespace-pre-wrap" />
            </div>
            {/* 展开/收起 */}
            {shouldCollapse && (
                <button className="text-xs text-blue-400 mt-1 hover:underline"
                    onClick={() => setExpanded(!expanded)}>
                    {expanded ? '收起' : `展开全部 (${lines.length} 行)`}
                </button>
            )}
            {/* 复制按钮 */}
            <button className="absolute top-2 right-10 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100
                text-xs text-gray-400 hover:text-white transition"
                onClick={() => navigator.clipboard.writeText(content)}>
                复制
            </button>
        </div>
    );
};
```

```typescript
// renderers/DiffRenderer.tsx — FileEditTool 专用渲染器
// 功能: 解析 unified diff 格式 + 增删行分色 + 行号显示
import React, { useMemo } from 'react';

interface DiffLine {
    type: 'add' | 'remove' | 'context' | 'header';
    content: string;
    oldLine?: number;
    newLine?: number;
}

function parseDiff(content: string): DiffLine[] {
    const lines = content.split('\n');
    const result: DiffLine[] = [];
    let oldLine = 0, newLine = 0;
    for (const line of lines) {
        if (line.startsWith('@@')) {
            const match = line.match(/@@ -(\d+).*\+(\d+)/);
            if (match) { oldLine = parseInt(match[1]) - 1; newLine = parseInt(match[2]) - 1; }
            result.push({ type: 'header', content: line });
        } else if (line.startsWith('+')) {
            newLine++;
            result.push({ type: 'add', content: line.slice(1), newLine });
        } else if (line.startsWith('-')) {
            oldLine++;
            result.push({ type: 'remove', content: line.slice(1), oldLine });
        } else {
            oldLine++; newLine++;
            result.push({ type: 'context', content: line.slice(1), oldLine, newLine });
        }
    }
    return result;
}

export const DiffRenderer: React.FC<{ content: string; filePath?: string }> = ({ content, filePath }) => {
    const diffLines = useMemo(() => parseDiff(content), [content]);
    const addCount = diffLines.filter(l => l.type === 'add').length;
    const removeCount = diffLines.filter(l => l.type === 'remove').length;

    return (
        <div className="rounded-md border border-gray-700 overflow-hidden">
            {/* 文件头 */}
            {filePath && (
                <div className="bg-gray-800 px-3 py-1.5 text-sm flex justify-between">
                    <span className="text-gray-300 font-mono">{filePath}</span>
                    <span className="text-xs">
                        <span className="text-green-400">+{addCount}</span>{' '}
                        <span className="text-red-400">-{removeCount}</span>
                    </span>
                </div>
            )}
            {/* Diff 行 */}
            <div className="font-mono text-sm overflow-x-auto">
                {diffLines.map((line, i) => (
                    <div key={i} className={`flex
                        ${line.type === 'add' ? 'bg-green-900/30' : ''}
                        ${line.type === 'remove' ? 'bg-red-900/30' : ''}
                        ${line.type === 'header' ? 'bg-blue-900/20 text-blue-400' : ''}`}>
                        <span className="w-10 text-right text-gray-600 select-none px-1 flex-shrink-0">
                            {line.oldLine || ''}
                        </span>
                        <span className="w-10 text-right text-gray-600 select-none px-1 flex-shrink-0">
                            {line.newLine || ''}
                        </span>
                        <span className={`w-4 text-center flex-shrink-0
                            ${line.type === 'add' ? 'text-green-400' : ''}
                            ${line.type === 'remove' ? 'text-red-400' : ''}`}>
                            {line.type === 'add' ? '+' : line.type === 'remove' ? '-' : ' '}
                        </span>
                        <span className="flex-1 whitespace-pre">{line.content}</span>
                    </div>
                ))}
            </div>
        </div>
    );
};
```

```typescript
// renderers/SearchResultRenderer.tsx — GrepTool 专用渲染器
// 功能: 文件路径可点击 + 关键词高亮 + 行号显示 + 分组
import React, { useMemo } from 'react';
import { sendToServer } from '@/hooks/useWebSocket';

interface GrepMatch {
    file: string;
    line: number;
    content: string;
    matchRanges?: [number, number][]; // 匹配位置
}

function parseGrepOutput(content: string): Map<string, GrepMatch[]> {
    const grouped = new Map<string, GrepMatch[]>();
    for (const line of content.split('\n')) {
        const match = line.match(/^(.+?):(\d+):(.*)$/);
        if (!match) continue;
        const [, file, lineNum, text] = match;
        if (!grouped.has(file)) grouped.set(file, []);
        grouped.get(file)!.push({ file, line: parseInt(lineNum), content: text });
    }
    return grouped;
}

export const SearchResultRenderer: React.FC<{ content: string; query?: string }> = ({ content, query }) => {
    const grouped = useMemo(() => parseGrepOutput(content), [content]);
    const totalMatches = Array.from(grouped.values()).reduce((sum, arr) => sum + arr.length, 0);

    const highlightMatch = (text: string) => {
        if (!query) return text;
        const regex = new RegExp(`(${query.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&')})`, 'gi');
        return text.replace(regex, '<mark class="bg-yellow-500/40 text-yellow-200">$1</mark>');
    };

    return (
        <div className="text-sm">
            <div className="text-xs text-gray-400 mb-2">
                {grouped.size} 个文件中找到 {totalMatches} 个匹配
            </div>
            {Array.from(grouped).map(([file, matches]) => (
                <div key={file} className="mb-3">
                    <button className="text-blue-400 hover:underline text-sm font-mono"
                        onClick={() => sendToServer('/app/command', {
                            command: 'open', args: `${file}:${matches[0].line}` })}>
                        {file}
                    </button>
                    <span className="text-gray-500 text-xs ml-2">({matches.length} 匹配)</span>
                    <div className="mt-1 bg-gray-900 rounded overflow-hidden">
                        {matches.map((m, i) => (
                            <div key={i} className="flex hover:bg-gray-800/50">
                                <span className="w-12 text-right text-gray-600 px-2 flex-shrink-0"
                                    >{m.line}</span>
                                <span className="flex-1 font-mono whitespace-pre"
                                    dangerouslySetInnerHTML={{ __html: highlightMatch(m.content) }} />
                            </div>
                        ))}
                    </div>
                </div>
            ))}
        </div>
    );
};
```

```typescript
// renderers/FileListRenderer.tsx — GlobTool 专用渲染器
// 功能: 树形文件列表 + 文件类型图标 + 可点击打开
import React, { useMemo } from 'react';

interface FileNode {
    name: string;
    path: string;
    isDir: boolean;
    children: FileNode[];
}

function buildTree(paths: string[]): FileNode[] {
    const root: FileNode = { name: '', path: '', isDir: true, children: [] };
    for (const path of paths) {
        const parts = path.split('/');
        let current = root;
        for (let i = 0; i < parts.length; i++) {
            const isLast = i === parts.length - 1;
            let child = current.children.find(c => c.name === parts[i]);
            if (!child) {
                child = { name: parts[i], path: parts.slice(0, i + 1).join('/'),
                    isDir: !isLast, children: [] };
                current.children.push(child);
            }
            current = child;
        }
    }
    return root.children;
}

const FileIcon: React.FC<{ isDir: boolean; name: string }> = ({ isDir, name }) => {
    if (isDir) return <span className="text-blue-400">📁</span>;
    const ext = name.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase();
    const icons: Record<string, string> = {
        java: '☕', ts: '🔵', tsx: '⚛️', py: '🐍', json: '📄',
        md: '📝', yaml: '⚙️', yml: '⚙️', xml: '📄', sql: '🗃️',
    };
    return <span>{icons[ext || ''] || '📄'}</span>;
};

const TreeNode: React.FC<{ node: FileNode; depth: number }> = ({ node, depth }) => (
    <div>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-1 py-0.5 hover:bg-gray-800/50 rounded px-1"
            style={{ paddingLeft: `${depth * 16}px` }}>
            <FileIcon isDir={node.isDir} name={node.name} />
            <span className={`text-sm font-mono ${node.isDir ? 'text-blue-300' : 'text-gray-300'}`}>
                {node.name}
            </span>
        </div>
        {node.children.map(child => (
            <TreeNode key={child.path} node={child} depth={depth + 1} />
        ))}
    </div>
);

export const FileListRenderer: React.FC<{ content: string }> = ({ content }) => {
    const paths = content.trim().split('\n').filter(Boolean);
    const tree = useMemo(() => buildTree(paths), [paths]);

    return (
        <div className="text-sm">
            <div className="text-xs text-gray-400 mb-2">{paths.length} 个文件</div>
            <div className="bg-gray-900 rounded p-2">
                {tree.map(node => <TreeNode key={node.path} node={node} depth={0} />)}
            </div>
        </div>
    );
};
```

### 4.2 流式渲染性能优化

**问题**: `messageStore.ts` L41-53 `appendStreamDelta` 每次 delta 触发 Immer produce，50-100 tokens/s 导致帧率下降。

**步骤 1**: Delta 批量合并 — requestAnimationFrame 节流
```typescript
// store/messageStore.ts — 替换原有 appendStreamDelta
// 原版问题: 每个 delta 触发一次 Immer produce + React 重渲染
// 优化: 使用 RAF 批量合并，降低到每帧更新一次

let deltaBuffer = '';
let rafId: number | null = null;

function flushDeltaBuffer() {
    if (!deltaBuffer) return;
    const chunk = deltaBuffer;
    deltaBuffer = '';
    rafId = null;
    // 单次 produce 合并所有累积的 delta
    set(state => {
        state.streamingContent += chunk;
    });
}

// 新版 appendStreamDelta:
appendStreamDelta: (delta: string) => {
    deltaBuffer += delta;
    if (rafId === null) {
        rafId = requestAnimationFrame(flushDeltaBuffer);
    }
},

// 流结束时刷新剩余缓冲:
finalizeStream: () => {
    if (rafId !== null) {
        cancelAnimationFrame(rafId);
        rafId = null;
    }
    flushDeltaBuffer(); // 确保最后一批 delta 不丢失
    set(state => {
        // 将 streamingContent 转化为正式消息
        if (state.streamingContent) {
            state.messages.push({
                type: 'assistant',
                uuid: crypto.randomUUID(),
                timestamp: Date.now(),
                content: [{ type: 'text', text: state.streamingContent }],
            } as Message);
            state.streamingContent = '';
        }
    });
},
```

**步骤 2**: StreamingText 独立状态 — `useSyncExternalStore` 避免全局重渲染
```typescript
// hooks/useStreamingText.ts — 将 streamingContent 提取为独立订阅
// 仅 StreamingText 组件订阅此状态，避免其他组件重渲染
import { useSyncExternalStore } from 'react';

// 外部存储 (绕过 Zustand，避免 Immer 开销)
let streamingContent = '';
let listeners = new Set<() => void>();

export const streamingStore = {
    getSnapshot: () => streamingContent,
    subscribe: (listener: () => void) => {
        listeners.add(listener);
        return () => listeners.delete(listener);
    },
    append: (delta: string) => {
        streamingContent += delta;
        // 不立即通知，在 RAF 中批量通知
    },
    flush: () => {
        listeners.forEach(l => l());
    },
    clear: () => {
        const content = streamingContent;
        streamingContent = '';
        listeners.forEach(l => l());
        return content;
    },
};

// RAF 批量通知
let notifyRafId: number | null = null;
export function appendStreamDelta(delta: string) {
    streamingStore.append(delta);
    if (notifyRafId === null) {
        notifyRafId = requestAnimationFrame(() => {
            notifyRafId = null;
            streamingStore.flush();
        });
    }
}

// React Hook:
// 技术栈适配: useSyncExternalStore 在 React 18 中需提供第三个参数 getServerSnapshot
// 用于 SSR (Server-Side Rendering) 场景。即使当前不用 SSR，React 18
// StrictMode 会检查此参数是否存在，缺少会在开发模式下报警。
// 原版 TS 使用 ink (CLI UI) 不涉及 SSR，但 Web 版必须考虑。
const EMPTY_SNAPSHOT = ''; // SSR 服务端快照 (streaming 在服务端永远为空)
export function useStreamingText(): string {
    return useSyncExternalStore(
        streamingStore.subscribe,
        streamingStore.getSnapshot,
        () => EMPTY_SNAPSHOT  // getServerSnapshot: SSR 兼容
    );
}
```

```typescript
// components/message/StreamingText.tsx — 仅订阅 streaming 状态
import { useStreamingText } from '@/hooks/useStreamingText';
import { MarkdownRenderer } from './MarkdownRenderer';

export const StreamingText: React.FC = () => {
    const text = useStreamingText();
    if (!text) return null;
    return (
        <div className="animate-pulse-subtle">
            <MarkdownRenderer content={text} />
            <span className="inline-block w-2 h-4 bg-blue-500 animate-blink ml-0.5" />
        </div>
    );
};
```

### 4.3 @文件附件功能

**步骤 1**: 前端 — `PromptInput.tsx` 添加 @触发逻辑
```typescript
// components/input/PromptInput.tsx — @文件触发逻辑

const [showFileComplete, setShowFileComplete] = useState(false);
const [fileQuery, setFileQuery] = useState('');
const [cursorPosition, setCursorPosition] = useState(0);

const handleInputChange = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLTextAreaElement>) => {
    const text = e.target.value;
    const cursor = e.target.selectionStart || 0;
    setText(text);
    setCursorPosition(cursor);

    // 检测 @ 触发 (对齐原版 @ 文件引用功能)
    const textBeforeCursor = text.slice(0, cursor);
    const atMatch = textBeforeCursor.match(/@([\w./\-]*)$/);
    if (atMatch) {
        setFileQuery(atMatch[1]);
        setShowFileComplete(true);
    } else {
        setShowFileComplete(false);
    }

    // 检测 / 命令触发
    if (text.startsWith('/') && !text.includes(' ')) {
        setCommandQuery(text.slice(1));
        setShowCommandComplete(true);
    } else {
        setShowCommandComplete(false);
    }
};

// 文件选中回调: 替换 @query 为完整路径
const handleFileSelect = (filePath: string) => {
    const textBeforeCursor = text.slice(0, cursorPosition);
    const atStart = textBeforeCursor.lastIndexOf('@');
    if (atStart >= 0) {
        const newText = text.slice(0, atStart) + '@' + filePath + ' ' + text.slice(cursorPosition);
        setText(newText);
    }
    setShowFileComplete(false);
};
```

**步骤 2**: 后端 — `FileController.java` 新增搜索端点
```java
// controller/FileController.java — 文件模糊搜索 API
@GetMapping("/api/files/search")
public ResponseEntity<List<FileSearchResult>> searchFiles(
        @RequestParam String q,
        @RequestParam(defaultValue = "20") int limit,
        @RequestParam(required = false) String workingDir) {
    String dir = workingDir != null ? workingDir : sessionContext.getWorkingDir();
    List<FileSearchResult> results = fileSearchService.fuzzySearch(q, dir, limit);
    return ResponseEntity.ok(results);
}

public record FileSearchResult(
    String path,       // 相对路径
    String name,       // 文件名
    String type,       // "file" | "directory"
    long size,         // 文件大小
    double score       // 匹配得分
) {}

// service/FileSearchService.java — 模糊搜索实现
// 技术栈适配说明:
// 1. Files.walk 不应使用 FOLLOW_LINKS —— 符号链接循环会导致无限递归
// 2. Files.walk 可能抛出 UncheckedIOException (权限不足等)，必须在 stream 内部处理
// 3. 深度限制通过参数传入，默认 8 层对大型 monorepo 可能不够
// 4. 原版 TS 使用 ripgrep (rg --files) 外部进程搜索，Java 版用 Files.walk 替代
@Service
public class FileSearchService {
    private static final Set<String> IGNORED_DIRS = Set.of(
        "node_modules", ".git", "target", "dist", "build", ".idea", "__pycache__");

    /**
     * @param maxDepth 遍历深度，默认 12 (原版 ripgrep 无深度限制，Java 需易控范围)
     */
    public List<FileSearchResult> fuzzySearch(String query, String rootDir, int limit, int maxDepth) {
        if (query == null || query.isBlank()) return List.of();
        Path root = Path.of(rootDir);
        // 技术栈适配: Files.walk 不使用 FOLLOW_LINKS 避免符号链接循环
        try (Stream<Path> paths = Files.walk(root, maxDepth)) {
            return paths
                .filter(p -> !isIgnored(p))
                .map(p -> {
                    try {
                        String relative = root.relativize(p).toString();
                        double score = fuzzyScore(query, relative);
                        return new FileSearchResult(
                            relative, p.getFileName().toString(),
                            Files.isDirectory(p) ? "directory" : "file",
                            safeSize(p), score);
                    } catch (UncheckedIOException e) {
                        // 技术栈适配: Files.walk 内部可能抛 UncheckedIOException
                        // (权限不足/文件被删除等)，跳过而非终止整个搜索
                        return null;
                    }
                })
                .filter(r -> r != null && r.score() > 0)
                .sorted(Comparator.comparingDouble(FileSearchResult::score).reversed())
                .limit(limit)
                .toList();
        } catch (IOException e) {
            log.warn("File search failed for root={}: {}", rootDir, e.getMessage());
            return List.of();
        }
    }

    // 重载: 默认深度
    public List<FileSearchResult> fuzzySearch(String query, String rootDir, int limit) {
        return fuzzySearch(query, rootDir, limit, 12);
    }

    private long safeSize(Path p) {
        try { return Files.isRegularFile(p) ? Files.size(p) : 0L; }
        catch (IOException e) { return 0L; }
    }

    // 模糊匹配算法: 子序列匹配 + 连续匹配加分
    private double fuzzyScore(String query, String target) {
        String lq = query.toLowerCase(), lt = target.toLowerCase();
        int qi = 0, score = 0, consecutive = 0;
        for (int ti = 0; ti < lt.length() && qi < lq.length(); ti++) {
            if (lt.charAt(ti) == lq.charAt(qi)) {
                qi++;
                consecutive++;
                score += consecutive * 2; // 连续匹配加分
                // 文件名匹配额外加分
                if (ti == 0 || target.charAt(ti - 1) == '/' || target.charAt(ti - 1) == '.')
                    score += 5;
            } else {
                consecutive = 0;
            }
        }
        return qi == lq.length() ? score : 0;
    }

    private boolean isIgnored(Path path) {
        for (Path part : path) {
            if (IGNORED_DIRS.contains(part.toString())) return true;
        }
        return false;
    }
}
```

**步骤 3**: 新建 `FileAutoComplete.tsx` 下拉组件
```typescript
// components/input/FileAutoComplete.tsx — 文件自动补全下拉
import React, { useState, useEffect, useRef } from 'react';

interface FileResult {
    path: string;
    name: string;
    type: 'file' | 'directory';
    score: number;
}

interface FileAutoCompleteProps {
    query: string;
    onSelect: (filePath: string) => void;
    onClose: () => void;
    position?: { top: number; left: number };
}

export const FileAutoComplete: React.FC<FileAutoCompleteProps> = ({
    query, onSelect, onClose, position,
}) => {
    const [results, setResults] = useState<FileResult[]>([]);
    const [selectedIndex, setSelectedIndex] = useState(0);
    const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
    const debounceRef = useRef<ReturnType<typeof setTimeout>>();

    // 防抖搜索
    useEffect(() => {
        if (!query) { setResults([]); return; }
        clearTimeout(debounceRef.current);
        debounceRef.current = setTimeout(async () => {
            setLoading(true);
            try {
                const res = await fetch(`/api/files/search?q=${encodeURIComponent(query)}&limit=15`);
                const data: FileResult[] = await res.json();
                setResults(data);
                setSelectedIndex(0);
            } catch { setResults([]); }
            setLoading(false);
        }, 150); // 150ms 防抖
        return () => clearTimeout(debounceRef.current);
    }, [query]);

    // 键盘导航
    useEffect(() => {
        const handler = (e: KeyboardEvent) => {
            switch (e.key) {
                case 'ArrowDown': e.preventDefault();
                    setSelectedIndex(i => Math.min(i + 1, results.length - 1)); break;
                case 'ArrowUp': e.preventDefault();
                    setSelectedIndex(i => Math.max(i - 1, 0)); break;
                case 'Enter': case 'Tab': e.preventDefault();
                    if (results[selectedIndex]) onSelect(results[selectedIndex].path); break;
                case 'Escape': onClose(); break;
            }
        };
        window.addEventListener('keydown', handler);
        return () => window.removeEventListener('keydown', handler);
    }, [results, selectedIndex, onSelect, onClose]);

    if (!results.length && !loading) return null;

    return (
        <div className="absolute z-50 bg-white dark:bg-gray-800 border rounded-lg shadow-xl
            max-h-64 overflow-y-auto w-80" style={position}>
            {loading && <div className="p-2 text-xs text-gray-400">搜索中...</div>}
            {results.map((r, i) => (
                <button key={r.path}
                    className={`w-full text-left px-3 py-1.5 flex items-center gap-2 text-sm
                        ${i === selectedIndex ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'hover:bg-gray-100 dark:hover:bg-gray-700'}`}
                    onClick={() => onSelect(r.path)}
                    onMouseEnter={() => setSelectedIndex(i)}>
                    <span>{r.type === 'directory' ? '📁' : '📄'}</span>
                    <span className="flex-1 font-mono truncate">{r.path}</span>
                </button>
            ))}
        </div>
    );
};
```

**涉及文件**:
- `frontend/src/components/input/PromptInput.tsx` — @触发逻辑
- `frontend/src/components/input/FileAutoComplete.tsx` — 新建下拉组件
- `backend/.../controller/FileController.java` — 新增搜索端点
- `backend/.../service/FileSearchService.java` — 新建模糊搜索服务

**优先级**: 🟡 P1

### 4.4 命令自动补全

**实施步骤**:

**步骤 1**: 命令数据源 — 从后端加载可用命令列表
```typescript
// types/command.ts — 命令类型定义
interface CommandItem {
    name: string;         // 命令名 (不含 /)
    description: string;  // 描述
    usage?: string;       // 用法示例
    category: 'builtin' | 'skill' | 'plugin'; // 来源
}

// store/commandStore.ts — 命令列表存储
import { create } from 'zustand';

interface CommandStoreState {
    commands: CommandItem[];
    loaded: boolean;
    loadCommands: () => Promise<void>;
}

export const useCommandStore = create<CommandStoreState>((set) => ({
    commands: [],
    loaded: false,
    loadCommands: async () => {
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/commands');
            const data: CommandItem[] = await res.json();
            set({ commands: data, loaded: true });
        } catch (err) {
            console.error('Failed to load commands:', err);
        }
    },
}));
```

**步骤 2**: 模糊匹配算法 + 排序
```typescript
// utils/fuzzyMatch.ts — 命令模糊匹配 (对齐原版命令补全逻辑)
function fuzzyMatch(query: string, items: CommandItem[]): CommandItem[] {
    if (!query) return items.slice(0, 10); // 无查询时显示前 10 个
    const lq = query.toLowerCase();
    return items
        .map(item => ({
            item,
            score: computeScore(lq, item.name.toLowerCase()),
        }))
        .filter(({ score }) => score > 0)
        .sort((a, b) => b.score - a.score)
        .map(({ item }) => item);
}

function computeScore(query: string, target: string): number {
    // 前缀匹配最高优先级
    if (target.startsWith(query)) return 100 + (target.length === query.length ? 50 : 0);
    // 包含匹配
    if (target.includes(query)) return 50;
    // 子序列匹配
    let qi = 0, score = 0;
    for (let ti = 0; ti < target.length && qi < query.length; ti++) {
        if (target[ti] === query[qi]) { qi++; score += 1; }
    }
    return qi === query.length ? score : 0;
}
```

**步骤 3**: 新建 `CommandAutoComplete.tsx` 组件
```typescript
// components/input/CommandAutoComplete.tsx
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { useCommandStore } from '@/store/commandStore';

interface CommandAutoCompleteProps {
    query: string;           // 不含前缀 /
    onSelect: (command: string) => void;
    onClose: () => void;
}

export const CommandAutoComplete: React.FC<CommandAutoCompleteProps> = ({
    query, onSelect, onClose,
}) => {
    const { commands, loaded, loadCommands } = useCommandStore();
    const [selectedIndex, setSelectedIndex] = useState(0);

    // 首次渲染时加载命令列表
    useEffect(() => { if (!loaded) loadCommands(); }, [loaded, loadCommands]);

    const filtered = fuzzyMatch(query, commands);

    // 键盘导航
    useEffect(() => {
        const handler = (e: KeyboardEvent) => {
            switch (e.key) {
                case 'ArrowDown': e.preventDefault();
                    setSelectedIndex(i => Math.min(i + 1, filtered.length - 1)); break;
                case 'ArrowUp': e.preventDefault();
                    setSelectedIndex(i => Math.max(i - 1, 0)); break;
                case 'Enter': case 'Tab': e.preventDefault();
                    if (filtered[selectedIndex]) onSelect('/' + filtered[selectedIndex].name); break;
                case 'Escape': onClose(); break;
            }
        };
        window.addEventListener('keydown', handler);
        return () => window.removeEventListener('keydown', handler);
    }, [filtered, selectedIndex, onSelect, onClose]);

    // query 变化时重置选中
    useEffect(() => setSelectedIndex(0), [query]);

    if (!filtered.length) return null;

    return (
        <div className="absolute bottom-full mb-1 left-0 z-50 bg-white dark:bg-gray-800
            border rounded-lg shadow-xl max-h-64 overflow-y-auto w-72">
            {filtered.map((cmd, i) => (
                <button key={cmd.name}
                    className={`w-full text-left px-3 py-2 flex flex-col
                        ${i === selectedIndex ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'hover:bg-gray-100 dark:hover:bg-gray-700'}`}
                    onClick={() => onSelect('/' + cmd.name)}
                    onMouseEnter={() => setSelectedIndex(i)}>
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                        <span className="font-mono font-semibold">/{cmd.name}</span>
                        <span className={`text-xs px-1 rounded
                            ${cmd.category === 'builtin' ? 'bg-blue-100 text-blue-800 dark:bg-blue-900 dark:text-blue-200'
                            : cmd.category === 'skill' ? 'bg-green-100 text-green-800 dark:bg-green-900 dark:text-green-200'
                            : 'bg-gray-100 text-gray-600'}`}>
                            {cmd.category}
                        </span>
                    </div>
                    <span className={`text-xs mt-0.5 ${i === selectedIndex ? 'text-blue-100' : 'text-gray-500'}`}>
                        {cmd.description}
                    </span>
                </button>
            ))}
        </div>
    );
};
```

**步骤 4**: 后端命令列表 API
```java
// controller/CommandController.java — 命令列表端点
@GetMapping("/api/commands")
public List<CommandInfo> listCommands() {
    return commandRegistry.getAll().stream()
        .filter(cmd -> cmd.isUserVisible())
        .map(cmd -> new CommandInfo(
            cmd.getName(), cmd.getDescription(),
            cmd.getUsage(), cmd.getCategory().name().toLowerCase()))
        .sorted(Comparator.comparing(CommandInfo::name))
        .toList();
}

public record CommandInfo(String name, String description, String usage, String category) {}
```

**涉及文件**:
- `frontend/src/components/input/PromptInput.tsx` — / 触发逻辑
- `frontend/src/components/input/CommandAutoComplete.tsx` — 新建
- `frontend/src/store/commandStore.ts` — 新建
- `frontend/src/utils/fuzzyMatch.ts` — 新建
- `backend/.../controller/CommandController.java` — 新增端点

**优先级**: 🟡 P1
